    jQuery(function($) {
        $(document).ready(function() {
			$("body ul.et_mobile_menu li.menu-item-has-children, body ul.et_mobile_menu  li.page_item_has_children").append('<a href="#" class="mobile-toggle"></a>');
   			$('.et_mobile_menu .menu-item-has-children>a').each(function(i) {
				const jq = $(this);
				jq.off("click");
				jq.click(function() {
					event.preventDefault();
					event.stopPropagation();
					$(this).parent('li').toggleClass('dt-open');
                	$(this).parent('li').find('ul.children').first().toggleClass('visible');
                	$(this).parent('li').find('ul.sub-menu').first().toggleClass('visible');
					return false;
   	       		});
			});
			
			$(".mobile-footer li.menu-item-has-children").append('<a href="#" class="mobile-toggle"></a>');
			$('.mobile-footer .menu-item-has-children>a').each(function(i) {
				const jq = $(this);
				jq.off("click touchstart mousedown");
				jq.on("click touchstart", function() {
					event.preventDefault();
					event.stopPropagation();
					$(this).parent('li').toggleClass('dt-open');
                	jq_ul_first_child = $(this).parent('li').find('ul.children').first();
					jq_ul_first_child.css('display') == 'none' ? jq_ul_first_child.css('display', 'block') : jq_ul_first_child.css('display', 'none'); 
					jq_ul_sub_first = $(this).parent('li').find('ul.sub-menu').first();
					jq_ul_sub_first.css('display') == 'none' ? jq_ul_sub_first.css('display', 'block') : jq_ul_sub_first.css('display', 'none');
					//this.parentElement.focus({"preventScroll": true, "focusVisible": true});
					return false;
   	       		});
			});
		});
    });
</script>

<p>All relevant DSPs are connected, the campaign monitoring is clear and offers many features.</p>
<p>The reporting functions are versatile and in-depth, and thus also provide support for analysis and problem-solving."</p>
